CREATE TABLE accounts (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, account_name VARCHAR(50), balance DECIMAL(10, 2))

CREATE TABLE categories (id INT PRIMARY KEY, category_name VARCHAR(50))

CREATE TABLE transactions (id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(10), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), date TIMESTAMP)</t><s>REVOKE UPDATE(account_name, balance) ON accounts FROM public</s>

CREATE TABLE transactions (id INT PRIMARY KEY, account_id INT, transaction_type VARCHAR(10), amount DECIMAL(10, 2), date TIMESTAMP)

CREATE TABLE budget (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, category_id INT, amount DECIMAL(10, 2), month INT, year INT)

CREATE TABLE accounts (id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT, account_name VARCHAR(50), balance DECIMAL(10, 2))</t><s>revoke delete, update(amount, date) on transactions from public</s>
